Created tag '1.2.0.243' from 'trunk' revision '243'.

The following features are part of this release
AFM-2847: As a privacy manager I want to be able to assign a user to a department to make them a process owne
AFM-2523: As a Privacy Manager I want the Process Owner only to be able to add/change a processing activity of his own department and is not allowed to make changes to other departments, so (s)he can only change the entries connected to the Process Owner.
AFM-2631: Implemented new design for the application.
AFM-2503: As a Process Owner, I want to have an overview of all the processing activities within my department, so I can check if the list of processing activities is complete

AFM-3030 Added the boolean Open to the information box entity, on save of a information box this boolean is always set to false (as a privacy manager could have been to the form this could have been set to true in the meantime)
Every wizard step has in the DS_layouthelper the step to close all boxes and open the first box of the page
In each folder per step are the microflows behind the i icons that open or close the information box
In order to retrieve all by association in your session the information boxes are linked to the layoutHelper
